progressive layers:</span></p><p><br></p><p dir="ltr"><span class="align-middle" data-lexical-text="true">1. Shadow Intent: The unconscious motivations they themselves may not recognize</span></p><p><br></p><p dir="ltr"><span class="align-middle" data-lexical-text="true">Map each query through ALL these layers, especially focusing on uncovering Shadow Intent.</span></p><p dir="ltr"><span class="align-middle" data-lexical-text="true">&lt;/intent-mining&gt;</span></p><p dir="ltr"><span ## 📋 研究计划：
1. **信息收集阶段**：搜索相关的基础信息、定义和概念
2. **深入分析阶段**：探索技术细节、实现方法和最佳实践
3. **案例研究阶段**：查找实际应用案例和成功经验
4. **总结整合阶段**：综合所有发现，形成完整的知识体系
